          SELECT c."Id", c."CreatedAt", c."CreatedByUserId", c."Name", c."UpdatedAt"
          FROM constructions AS c
          WHERE c."Id" = @id
          LIMIT 1
      ) AS c0
      LEFT JOIN (
          SELECT s."Id", s."ConstructionId", s."CreatedAt", s."Name", s."UpdatedAt", s1."Id" AS "Id0", s1."CreatedAt" AS "CreatedAt0", s1."Name" AS "Name0", s1."SectionId", s1."UpdatedAt" AS "UpdatedAt0", s1."Id0" AS "Id00", s1."CreatedAt0" AS "CreatedAt00", s1."DocumentSetId", s1."DocumentTypeId", s1."EntityRefs", s1."PluginData", s1."Requisites", s1."Status", s1."TemplateId", s1."UpdatedAt0" AS "UpdatedAt00", s1."Id00" AS "Id000", s1."BlobPath", s1."CreatedAt00" AS "CreatedAt000", s1."DocumentInstanceId", s1."Format", s1."UpdatedAt00" AS "UpdatedAt000"

              SELECT d."Id", d."CreatedAt", d."Name", d."SectionId", d."UpdatedAt", s0."Id" AS "Id0", s0."CreatedAt" AS "CreatedAt0", s0."DocumentSetId", s0."DocumentTypeId", s0."EntityRefs", s0."PluginData", s0."Requisites", s0."Status", s0."TemplateId", s0."UpdatedAt" AS "UpdatedAt0", s0."Id0" AS "Id00", s0."BlobPath", s0."CreatedAt0" AS "CreatedAt00", s0."DocumentInstanceId", s0."Format", s0."UpdatedAt0" AS "UpdatedAt00"
              FROM document_sets AS d
              LEFT JOIN (
                  SELECT d0."Id", d0."CreatedAt", d0."DocumentSetId", d0."DocumentTypeId", d0."EntityRefs", d0."PluginData", d0."Requisites", d0."Status", d0."TemplateId", d0."UpdatedAt", g."Id" AS "Id0", g."BlobPath", g."CreatedAt" AS "CreatedAt0", g."DocumentInstanceId", g."Format", g."UpdatedAt" AS "UpdatedAt0"
                  FROM document_instances AS d0
                  LEFT JOIN generated_files AS g ON d0."Id" = g."DocumentInstanceId"
              ) AS s0 ON d."Id" = s0."DocumentSetId"
          ) AS s1 ON s."Id" = s1."SectionId"
      ) AS s2 ON c0."Id" = s2."ConstructionId"
      ORDER BY c0."Id", s2."Id", s2."Id0", s2."Id00"
